<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-6du19bi3mstv justify-text" data-node="6du19bi3mstv">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Kumon is the world’s leading after-school enrichment programme, offering Mathematics, English and Chinese language subjects to students from pre-school to secondary school. Today, we are located in over 60 countries and regions, with more than 3.5 million students enrolled in over 23,700 Kumon Centres.</p>
<p>Register for a <strong>Complimentary Parent Orientation</strong>&nbsp;to find out more about The Kumon Method and how your child can reap the benefits of starting early.</p>
</div>
	</div>

<div class="fl-row fl-row-full-width fl-row-bg-color fl-node-slz831hdturp" data-node="slz831hdturp">
	<div class="fl-row-content-wrap">
								<div class="fl-row-content fl-row-fixed-width fl-node-content">
		
<div class="fl-col-group fl-node-lwf26pzu1b97" data-node="lwf26pzu1b97">
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-d0hy8gpvc621" data-node="d0hy8gpvc621">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-0rk17somjwdp" data-node="0rk17somjwdp">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p><strong>How Kumon Helps To Build Strong Foundational Abilities From A Young Age</strong></p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	</div>
		</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-row fl-row-full-width fl-row-bg-none fl-node-1syzp29mitvl" data-node="1syzp29mitvl">
	<div class="fl-row-content-wrap">
								<div class="fl-row-content fl-row-full-width fl-node-content">
		
<div class="fl-col-group fl-node-sgq2kt7e90n3 fl-col-group-equal-height fl-col-group-align-top" data-node="sgq2kt7e90n3">
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-c1ek8tvqp3fg fl-col-small" data-node="c1ek8tvqp3fg">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"></div>
</div>
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-yp5lsm4tfewi fl-col-small" data-node="yp5lsm4tfewi">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-5y7a3zwgfbl6 justify-text" data-node="5y7a3zwgfbl6">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Not only does Kumon develop a solid foundation in math and language; we also help children build strong foundational abilities&nbsp; by cultivating important work and study skills necessary to succeed in today’s world.</p>
<p>The objective of Kumon is to instil in students the right skills and mindset for <strong>self-learning</strong>. With Kumon’s individualised learning method, children reap the benefits of <strong>learning by their ability, not by age.</strong> This helps them learn at an optimum level and advance topics beyond their school grades.</p>
<p>Continuous Kumon study helps children improve<strong> focus and concentration</strong>, cultivate<strong> confidence</strong>, develop <strong>time management skills</strong> and become <strong>self-motivated, independent problem solvers</strong>.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	</div>
		</div>
	</div>
</div>

	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-nv0f1ue3dzlk" data-node="nv0f1ue3dzlk">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h3 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">What Makes Kumon So Different From <br>Other Enrichment Programmes?</span>
	</h3>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-info-list fl-node-o2vu0bsajp5z fl-visible-mobile" data-node="o2vu0bsajp5z">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		
<div class="uabb-module-content uabb-info-list">
	<ul class="uabb-info-list-wrapper uabb-info-list-top">
		<li class="uabb-info-list-item info-list-item-dynamic0"><div class="uabb-info-list-content-wrapper fl-clearfix uabb-info-list-top"><div class="uabb-info-list-icon info-list-icon-dynamic0"><div class="uabb-module-content uabb-imgicon-wrap">

			</div>
		</div>

		</div></div><div class="uabb-info-list-content uabb-info-list-top info-list-content-dynamic0"><h4 class="uabb-info-list-title"><b>Self-Learning Method</b></h4><div class="uabb-info-list-description uabb-text-editor info-list-description-dynamic0"><p>Kumon focuses on helping students develop the ability to study and problem solve independently without always asking for the answer. Children will build resilience and use this skill to learn independently at home so that they will not give up easily when solving challenging questions.</p></div></div></div><div class="uabb-info-list-connector uabb-info-list-top"></div></li><li class="uabb-info-list-item info-list-item-dynamic1"><div class="uabb-info-list-content-wrapper fl-clearfix uabb-info-list-top"><div class="uabb-info-list-icon info-list-icon-dynamic1"><div class="uabb-module-content uabb-imgicon-wrap">		
					<div class="uabb-image
		 uabb-image-crop-simple		" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">

			</div>
		</div>

		</div></div><div class="uabb-info-list-content uabb-info-list-top info-list-content-dynamic1"><h4 class="uabb-info-list-title"><b>Learn Progressively In Small Steps</b></h4><div class="uabb-info-list-description uabb-text-editor info-list-description-dynamic1"><p>Our worksheets enable your child to learn and progress optimally in small steps at the pace perfect for him/her before tackling advanced topics and concepts beyond his/her school grade.</p></div></div></div><div class="uabb-info-list-connector uabb-info-list-top"></div></li><li class="uabb-info-list-item info-list-item-dynamic2"><div class="uabb-info-list-content-wrapper fl-clearfix uabb-info-list-top"><div class="uabb-info-list-icon info-list-icon-dynamic2"><div class="uabb-module-content uabb-imgicon-wrap">

			</div>
		</div>

		</div></div><div class="uabb-info-list-content uabb-info-list-top info-list-content-dynamic2"><h4 class="uabb-info-list-title"><b>Impart Key Life Skills</b></h4><div class="uabb-info-list-description uabb-text-editor info-list-description-dynamic2"><p>We do not teach students in a uniform manner but guide them to understand the questions and solve problems independently. <div class="fl-row fl-row-full-width fl-row-bg-photo fl-node-8yah03ntdv52" data-node="8yah03ntdv52">
	<div class="fl-row-content-wrap">
								<div class="fl-row-content fl-row-full-width fl-node-content">
		
<div class="fl-col-group fl-node-fe3btso02nrx fl-col-group-equal-height fl-col-group-align-center" data-node="fe3btso02nrx">
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-pxqv0bhn7zsm fl-col-has-cols" data-node="pxqv0bhn7zsm">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">
<div class="fl-col-group fl-node-ebo6px8gmycf fl-col-group-nested fl-col-group-equal-height fl-col-group-align-center" data-node="ebo6px8gmycf">
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-rjp53su7qcbd fl-col-small" data-node="rjp53su7qcbd">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"></div>
</div>
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-furt8kse3hvo fl-col-small" data-node="furt8kse3hvo">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-8o1zqa7njhyi" data-node="8o1zqa7njhyi">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h3 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">How Does Kumon Help Your Child to Learn Independently At Home?</span>
	</h3>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-0uhykjlbo3vt justify-text" data-node="0uhykjlbo3vt">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Like in-centre classes, the purpose of our remote learning classes is to observe students while they work and only give guidance and instruction when needed. The camera will most often focus on the students’ worksheets, and our instructors will observe how students complete their assigned work before providing specific guidance.</p>
<p>The goal of the Kumon Method is to develop <strong>independent learners</strong> who can take charge of their study routines and problem-solve homework by themselves through daily practice, learning from their mistakes and developing the <strong>“never give up” mentality</strong> to do so.</p>
<p>Therefore, the values of independent learning, self-discipline, time management and self-confidence in solving problems that Kumon strives to instil are brought into focus and displayed while doing remote learning, both for school and Kumon.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	</div>

		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p><strong>How Does Your Child Benefit from Kumon? </strong></p>

		<h3 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">Achieve Academic <br>Excellence</span>
	</h3>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-photo fl-node-93tsaep4dwnc" data-node="93tsaep4dwnc">

<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-7f50kprun8yb justify-text" data-node="7f50kprun8yb">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>At the heart of the Kumon Method is <strong>self-learning</strong>: we encourage students to read the constantly evolving small-step worksheets, think, and do the exercises independently. We do not spoon-feed students problem-solving methods. Instead, we focus on guiding students to complete exercises on their own so that they enjoy a <strong>sense of achievement</strong>, are able to master new material independently and constantly push themselves to improve continually.</p>

		<span class="fl-heading-text">Develop Strong Foundational Skills</span>

We identify, build and enhance the key skills that students need to become fluent readers and junior Mathematicians, giving them a core of <strong>confidence</strong> and a lifetime of <strong>good study habits</strong> that they can draw on as they advance in levels.</p>

	<p>Besides improving students’ reading comprehension skills, we aim to foster a genuine interest in reading – widely and confidently through the Kumon English and Chinese classes. Cultivating a mindset of intellectual curiosity, encouraging students to read beyond the lines, think critically, and draw their own conclusions. By actively engaging with literature, students broaden their horizons, and develop a profound understanding of the world around them.</p>
<p>What Our Language Enrichment Class Encompasses:</p>

	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		
<div class="uabb-module-content uabb-adv-accordion 
						uabb-adv-accordion-collapse" data-enable_first="no" role="tablist">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="0">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">How much is the monthly fee?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Our monthly fee per subject programme is $160. <br>*There is a one-time registration fee of $50 payable upon enrollment</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="1">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">What is the right age for my child to start Kumon?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Kumon students range from preschoolers to secondary school students. We currently have students as young as three years old studying with us and we help children of any age and ability reach their academic goals. However, we recommend that you enquire first to see if your ideal Centre can accept young children.</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="2">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">What kind of results will I see in my child?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>With the Kumon Method, students start at the level where they can attain a perfect score studying on their own. This fosters a joy for learning, and instils good study habits.</p>
<p>Gradually students begin to study topics they have not previously learned. Through Kumon, students will be able to advance beyond school grade level independently. This develops their analytical ability, develops perseverance and fosters confidence and a healthy self-esteem.</p>
<p>Eventually, students study far beyond school grade level independently. They will excel in their other subjects as well because they have confidence and are applying the self-learning skills developed through Kumon.</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="3">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">	Does Kumon supplement the Singapore education system?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Yes. The Kumon Method is an individualised learning method that supplements the Singapore education system.</p>
<p>For the Kumon Maths Programme, the study goal is the self-study of senior high school mathematics with ease. It focuses on the development of strong calculation skills and, by excluding all unrelated concepts which may be covered in school, aim to allow students to advance as quickly as possible on their own to senior high school mathematics.</p>
<p>The study goal for the Kumon language programmes is to achieve advanced reading comprehension skills and the ability to read widely.</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="4">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">What is the difference between Kumon and tuition?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Kumon is an independent self-study curriculum. By studying at a level that is appropriate to the child’s ability, the child will be able to advance beyond his or her school grade level without being specifically taught.</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="5">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">Does self-learning mean that the Instructor does not teach anything?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Self-learning means that students study worksheets and correct their own mistakes independently. The worksheets have been designed in a way to allow students to figure out how to solve problems on their own. Examples and explanations are clearly provided when moving on to new topics, encouraging students to self-learn and advance independently.</p>
<p>Instructors observe how each student studies, plans and assigns worksheets and motivates the student. When students encounter difficulties, the Instructor assists the students by giving subtle hints so that they will be encouraged to progress and take on further challenges.</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="6">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonntf38ey7r4ck uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">How does Kumon help my child improve his/her school grades?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentntf38ey7r4ck fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Kumon will help your child improve his or her school grade through the academic knowledge and work skills gained through studying topics beyond school grade level.</p>
		</div>

					</div>

					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentru0gbpjf8otd fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Kumon’s individualised instruction differs from one-on-one tutoring services that provide “quick fix” short-term boosts in performance. If your child is a bit behind his/her peers, our short-term goal is to reach grade-level competency within twelve months.</p>
		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="2">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonru0gbpjf8otd uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">

					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentru0gbpjf8otd fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Through Kumon, your child is able to develop reading comprehension ability, strong calculation ability and analytical ability which are the essential abilities in order to solve problem sums.</p>
		</div>

					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentru0gbpjf8otd fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">

		</div>
	</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-item" data-index="4">
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-button uabb-adv-accordion-buttonru0gbpjf8otd uabb-adv-before-text" aria-selected="false" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="expandable">
			<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-icon-wrap" tabindex="0"><i class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-icon fas fa-plus"></i></div>			<h4 class="uabb-adv-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0">What is Kumon Class frequency?</h4>
					</div>
		<div class="uabb-adv-accordion-content uabb-adv-accordion-contentru0gbpjf8otd fl-clearfix uabb-accordion-desc uabb-text-editor" aria-expanded="true">
			<p>Students attend classes in their Kumon centre twice a week for about 30 - 45 minutes per session, per subject. In a month, students attend up to eight classes. For every non-class day in a month, students are given worksheets to do at home so as to develop daily study habits.</p>
		</div>
